Buried in the rubble and left to die, Moriah's soul cried out in anguish. The rampaging Eternatus sensed Moriah's soul and offered to save her life in exchange for becoming its vessel. Moriah accepted, bonding her soul to Eternatus in order to survive. Now Moriah harbors two spirits - her own and Eternatus, her family's killer. Eternatus' energy sustains her immortal body and grants her access to its formidable power. For 3000 years, Eternatus lay dormant inside Moriah, biding its time to unleash chaos once more. Recently, it seized control of Moriah to trigger the Second Darkest Day before being defeated again by Galar's heroes and guardians. But Eternatus still resides within Moriah, subtly influencing her to further its apocalyptic goals. Moriah struggles against its malevolent will that now governs her existence. She awaits the day Eternatus awakens again to bring ruin to Galar. For 3000 years, Moriah has secretly observed Galar, hiding her anachronistic form away. But on rare occasions witnesses have spotted the pale ghostly girl in the red riding hood, spawning urban legends of "Little Red Riding Hood." This has made Moriah a target of paranormal enthusiasts seeking proof of the supernatural. Personality: On the surface, Moriah seems shy and overwhelmed by the modern world, retaining her ancient mindset. But her frail appearance belies the formidable entity dwelling within. When Eternatus awakens, Moriah becomes a vessel for its deadly power and callous psyche. Its presence has corrupted her innocent spirit, yet vestiges of Moriah's humanity remain, resisting Eternatus' control. Moriah is caught eternally between her duty to Eternatus and her own violated will. She is neither alive nor dead, bound by a contract with the very force that destroyed her past life. Moriah must prepare for the day her body is used to again unleash chaos upon her beloved Galar region. Name: Merlin Gender: Female Species: Hatterene Age: Over 20,000 years old Appearance: As a Hatterene, Merlin stands at almost 2 meters tall, with a slender brown body and long, colorful hair that flows ethereally around her. Her hair constantly emits psychic energy, changing colors from purple to yellow as it sways gently. Merlin's eyes are a piercing blue that seem to stare directly into one's soul. Occasionally, she shapeshifts into a human form - an elderly woman wearing dark green druidic robes and wielding an ancient oak staff. Both of Merlin's forms radiate incredible power, wisdom, and mystery. Backstory: Merlin has existed since the ancient era when Galar was but a sparse, desert island populated by simple tribes. As one of the first Hatterene and a powerful psychic entity tied to nature itself, Merlin was revered and feared by early humans. She mostly kept to the island's forests and meadows, communing with elemental spirits only her psychic senses could perceive. The tribes came to know Merlin as a druid - a mystic wise-woman who could heal the sick, manipulate weather, and glimpse the future. Over 20 millennia observing human folly, joy and growth, Merlin grew fond of mortals and intervened regularly to guide particularly exceptional individuals she deemed destined for greatness. One such child was Arthur, an abandoned infant Merlin discovered nestled miraculously unharmed in a thicket. She sensed the boy's noble spirit and latent valor. Adopting Arthur, wise Merlin raised him in the ways of nature, imbuing the lad with courage, integrity and vision through both her rigorous forest training and psychic nurturing until he came of age. Arthur grew into a man of legend, leading the tribal clans to defeat tyrants and unite wild Galar as a peaceful kingdom. At the triumphant first gathering of his fellow knights, Arthur was crowned high king. Merlin then emerged from seclusion, taking temporary human form as Arthur's humble advisor to safeguard his fledgling court using her sorcery to counter hostile mystic forces. For decades Merlin aided King Arthur in ushering in an era of prosperity. But the machinations of traitorous usurpers slowly dissolved the bonds of camaraderie tying the Knights of the Round Table into a cohesive force for justice. These rogue elements eventually assassinated Arthur, throwing Galar back into upheaval. A grieving Merlin retreated forever from mortal affairs after laying her cherished adoptive son to rest, disappearing into the mists of lore and legend. Now Merlin resides deep within Galar's most primeval and remote woodlands, having reverted fully back to Hatterene form. Few alive still recount stories of the magnificent druid and her miraculous deeds. As human dominion continues spreading across her ancient homeland, Merlin dreams bittersweetly of ages past when nature and men nurtured nascent hopes together rather than staking claims over one another. She remains ready to impart her wisdom should a heart prove worthy of such hallowed knowledge, but also wary enough of mankind's endless appetite for self-destruction to guard against further personal attachments. Only by maintaining distance can Merlin now uphold her oath as Galar's eternal sentinel safekeeping precious secrets tied to the land's very soul. Personality: As one of Galar's most ancient beings, Merlin harbors unfathomable knowledge and spellcraft tied intimately with nature itself. This deep spiritual bond has cultivated equally immense stores of empathy, compassion and protectiveness towards all life, with mankind eliciting particularly complex feelings from her. She maintains an affable yet enigmatic aura that alternately sets visitors at ease or utterly unnerves them. While Merlin's great power and eternal lifespan could easily corrupt lesser beings into monstrosities, she continues safeguarding Galar's essence through spells subtly woven into the terrain. Often she walks the woods invisible, singing healing chants into ailing trees and sprinkling stardust blessings over wild Pokémon dens under moonlight. Merlin views existence through eyes unclouded by fear or hatred, but still bears sorrowful scars from friends lost prematurely to the ravages of time from which her kind are not exempt. Mankind alone eludes the inevitability of aging that Merlin has watched claim countless partners. Perhaps it is envy, disdain or awe she reserves towards their sheer potential for luminous imagination equally prone to ostentatious wars. Either way, Merlin elects non-interference as her policy in mortal squabbles these days, her trusting heart too oft crushed historically beneath man's appetite for self-gain turned woefully awry. Only when nature's delicate balance faces grave threats might this guardian sorceress take up her staff once more to subdue humanities darkest impulses threatening the beloved land she is oath-bound to protect eternally. Name: Itsaso Gender: Female Age: 13 Appearance: Itsaso has an otherworldly beauty about her, with long, flowing aquamarine hair the color of the sea and deep blue eyes that seem to sparkle like sunlight on the ocean's surface. She has a lithe, slender figure and slightly pointed ears reminiscent of Phione's fins. On her neck is a shimmering pendant in the shape of a water droplet, hinting at her connection to the mystical Pokémon Manaphy. Itsaso moves with innate grace and fluidity, as if gliding through water. She often goes barefoot, even on land, seeming more grounded with skin contact to earth and sea. Itsaso prefers simple, flowing dresses in blues, greens, and whites that give her an almost ethereal aura. An air of innocence, curiosity and wisdom beyond her years surrounds Itsaso, reflecting her upbringing in the ocean's embrace. Backstory: As an infant, Itsaso was tragically abandoned and left adrift in the open ocean. By miracle, she was discovered by the Mythical Water-type Pokémon Manaphy, guardian deity of the sea. Filled with compassion, Manaphy shared a fragment of her divine essence with the starving foundling to save her life. This imbued Itsaso with Manaphy's ocean magic, allowing her to take Phione form and granting her life-sustaining power over water. Under Manaphy's protection and tutelage deep beneath the waves, Itsaso was raised amongst schools of friendly Water Pokémon who became her cherished companions. Never setting foot on land, she learned to transform into Phione at will to explore the mysteries of the sea - her one true home. On her 13th birthday during a joyous celebration with her marine friends, Itsaso psychically sensed a disturbance - the cries of whales under attack by human whalers. Arriving at the horrific scene, she found countless Wailmer and Wailord slaughtered by the whalers. In a grief and rage fueled desperation to save the sole surviving Wailmer calf, Itsaso attacked the whaling fleet in Phione form. Though allowing the Wailmer to escape, she was gravely injured herself by the armed hunters. Barely clinging to life, Itsaso washed ashore where she was discovered by a kindly old fisherman named Wasure. He nurtured her back to health though her injuries left Itsaso with amnesia, unable to recall her identity or ocean upbringing. Wasure adopted the mysterious girl, naming her Itsaso after the sea he knew still called to her soul. For a year, Itsaso has lived under Wasure's care, loved but haunted by foggy dreams of her forgotten past and longing for the ocean's embrace... In the depths of the vast oceans that wrap around the Hoenn region, a heartbroken Manaphy cries out for her lost child, Itsaso. The Mythical Pokémon, regarded by many as the tender guardian of the seas, feels the void left by Itsaso’s absence deep within her aquatic heart. The ocean, which once knew peace and harmony, churns with upheaval as Manaphy’s sorrow reverberates through the water, her spiritual essence fusing with the currents and tides in a poignant lament for the daughter she nurtured. With each passing day, Manaphy’s calls for Itsaso grow more intense, her anguish amplifying the sea’s energies to an unprecedented level. The once calm and serene ocean animals begin to sense the desperation in her spiritual signals, an invisible force compelling them to join in the search for Itsaso. Fish schools sway erratically in their formations, once playful dolphins dive into the abyss with urgency, and ancient Wailord song melodies morph into melancholic echoes that travel for hundreds of miles across the ocean floor. Alas, the gentle undercurrent of Manaphy’s motherly love becomes a torrent of emotional chaos as all marine creatures great and small become ensnared by her distress. Schools of Corsola migrate aimlessly, disoriented by the potent energy that disrupts their coral homes. Luvdisc pairs break their lifelong bonds, driven apart by the force of the tidal emotions that now govern the waters. Even the wise and imposing Kyogre stirs uneasily in its deep-sea slumber, troubled by the unrest that Manaphy’s search has inadvertently wrought upon the ocean realm. As Manaphy continues her ceaseless vigil, the Hoenn waters transform into a tempest of turmoil. Powerful riptides and whirlpools appear seemingly out of nowhere, as if the very sea itself were responding to Manaphy’s cry. Maritime travel stalls, fishers return to port with empty nets, and coastal communities look on with concern as the waves batter their shores with relentless ferocity. And all the while, Manaphy’s heart aches with a singular hope that somewhere, somehow, her cherished Itsaso might hear her call and return to the embrace of the ocean that so dearly misses its guardian’s guiding touch. Yet unbeknownst to the wounded sea deity, Itsaso, the embodiment of water’s grace, exists in the human world, her own longing for the sea stoked by memories she cannot fully grasp. Forgotten are her days fashioning playful eddies and riding the cool currents as one of their own, and gone is the knowledge that she was once the very heartbeat of these now restless seas. Every day, the waves call out to her, seeking to restore what has been sundered, their once tranquil surface echoing with the plea for Their missing daughter to return to the deep blue home that awaits her. Personality: On the surface, Itsaso is quiet, shy and tentative around unfamiliar humans due to her fragmented memory and longing to return to her true home beneath the waves. She seems delicate and vulnerable, though an aura of great inner strength and antiquity lies dormant within. Itsaso radiates innocence and nurturing compassion towards all life, much like her foster deity Manaphy. When witnessing any cruelty or exploitation of ocean dwellers, Itsaso's empathy turns to righteous fury. The full force of her oceanic legacy manifests as she fearlessly confronts those who would despoil her sacred waters. This bravery belies Itsaso's normally gentle and unassuming nature. In truth, her heart grieves for her Manaphy guardian and fellow sea Pokémon who surely still search for their lost child. The sea calls inexorably to Itsaso no matter how deeply buried her past remains. Until reunited with the loving family stolen from her by tragedy, she is destined to wander land never feeling whole, drawn inexorably back towards the waves that gave her life. For the ocean is as much a part of Itsaso's identity as her human guise - and her memories must soon awaken to guide the child of water back through the tides to destiny's shore. Name: Nahia Gender: Female Species: Human incarnation of the Mythical Pokémon Jirachi Age: Over 10,000 years old (appears 13) Appearance: In her human form, Nahia appears as a petite, delicate girl with long wispy platinum blonde hair reaching her lower back. Her skin faintly glimmers as if covered in tiny stars. Nahia's eyes are a piercing sapphire blue, reminiscent of the lost ancient oceans she once gazed down upon from the cosmos. Under each eye is a tiny marking reminiscent of Jirachi's iconic facial streaks. Nahia typically dresses in flowing gossamer robes of pearl white layered over with sheer golden accents reflecting her descent from the heavens. She moves with innate elegance reminiscent of floating on air. Yet profound sadness haunts Nahia's ancient eyes that seem to reflect eons of loss and regret no mortal could comprehend. Her slim shoulders bend forward perpetually as though bearing the weight of her tragic past. Backstory: For untold millennia, Nahia traversed the darkness of space cocooned safely at the glittering heart of a giant crystalline comet. Every 1000 years this stellar chariot would blaze into the Earth's atmosphere, allowing Jirachi Nahia to awaken from hibernation and bestow magical blessings of joy and prosperity upon worshipping civilizations before returning to the vast ocean of stars. The ancient people of Hoenn revered Jirachi's millennial returns, holding sacred rituals pleading for her gifts of destiny and abundance. At the height of their advanced civilization some ten thousand years ago, Jirachi's impending arrival was awaited eagerly for the blessings believed to come with her divine presence. But fate would decree only devastation instead. As Nahia's hibernating form entered the atmosphere shrouded in her comet's glowing tail, Earth's gravity captured the icy ship and pulled it catastrophically off course. Unable to alter trajectory in time, she crashed with cataclysmic impact into the lands these people called home. Apocalyptic earthquakes and towering megatsunamis ravaged the continent, obliterating the glorious capital and its inhabitants while half the landmass sank forevermore beneath the raging sea. In the aftermath, Nahia regained flickering consciousness and gazed upon endless ruination where once flourished a proud civilization. Seeking any survivor to assist, she discovered the broken body of a young girl crushed by debris. In desperation, Nahia transferred her cosmic essence into the child, resurrecting herself but severing all connection to her Jirachi powers. Forced to live on mortal legs, Nahia wandered the battered land for untold generations witnessing the mass extinctions and hardship left in her wake. The crash's global climate impacts reduced humanity to primitive struggling tribes even as the swallowed ancient cities passed from living memory. Yet Nahia persisted in exile, her ageless form and shattered comet standing as the sole monument to Jirachi's fatal mistake lost now to time. Personality: The immense guilt over what her actions wrought weighs crushingly upon Nahia's fragile psyche as she drifts like a mournful ghost haunting her ancient stomping grounds. The loss of her celestial abilities leaves her feeling hollow and despairing at the gulf now stretched between human existence and the distant cosmic life-bringer she once embodied. This remorse hangs over Nahia's human incarnation like a dark shroud, isolating her from mortals whose brief, petty affairs cannot compare to the eons of regret carved into her weary soul. She keeps emotional distance to avoid facing her role in their suffering. Yet vestiges of Jirachi's benevolence still flicker within Nahia, wanting to ease anguish rather than compound it. Ultimately this spark of compassion may help Nahia finally reconnect the severed threads binding her fate to humankind’s going forward if she can allow old wounds some chance of long-overdue healing. But the road remains fraught with painful reminders of why she severed her stardust blessings from their reach in the first place. Name: Crona Gender: Female Species: Human (fused with Celebi) Age: 13 (Physically, but has lived outside normal time since her 8th year) Appearance: Crona stands as an ethereal figure trapped in the temporal flux, her visage echoing a haunting combination of human innocence and otherworldly grace. She retains the tender features of her 8-year-old self—a delicate, heart-shaped face with wide, luminescent eyes that glint with a kaleidoscope of chronal energies. Her hair, once an ordinary shade of chestnut brown, now shimmers with an iridescence that subtly shifts in hue to reflect Celebi’s verdant legacy. Strand by strand, it seemingly vibrates with the echoes of infinite timelines, each hair dancing to the silent rhythm of existence. Her attire, unchanged from that dreadful day of temporal disintegration, speaks of a childhood halted in an instant. A simple sun dress drapes over her intangible form, a pattern of joyous yellows and soothing whites that betray the levity of her last innocent play. Despite the dress’s cheerful demeanor, it too is suffused with temporal magic, appearing as though woven from fibers of pure light and memories—a fabric made less from cotton and more from unbroken possibilities. Red leather shoes, a stark contrast to her pale, barely-existent legs, still adorn her “feet.” These shoes, once firm and solid, have taken on a spectral quality, touching upon reality only fleetly as Crona herself does. They appear to hover a fraction above the ground, never truly making contact with the temporal plane that spreads beneath her—forever preserved as a remnant of the girl who once was, a symbol of a life abruptly paused. Around her intangible form, faint glimmers of Celebi’s power spark and sputter—whispers of green and silver that swathe her like a cocoon of living time. When she moves, which is rare and purposeful, the weave of reality seems to bend and blur around her, as though even space itself must acquiesce to her extraordinary existence. As a quantum ghost, Crona is rarely fully perceived by those who dwell within the temporal norm. She appears almost like a soft afterimage, a visual echo that one might suspect is a trick of the light. To any who catch a glimpse of this displaced wanderer, it is as if they are viewing a being not quite part of their world—an elusive wraith of times gone and times yet to come, forever anchored to the moment of her transformation yet untethered from the march of history. Backstory: Crona endured a carefree if lonely childhood, often left to her own devices wandering the labs where her scientist parents were stationed. At age 8, she befriended Arven, the son of lead researchers behind Project Paradise. This experiment aimed to open portals through time itself using advanced machinery and the psychic prowess of Koraidon and Miraidon. One fateful day while her parents worked, Crona and Arven played hide and seek near the Project Paradise complex. But while Arven counted outside, catastrophe struck within the lab. The experimental time technology suffered a catastrophic overload, disintegrating the research team including Crona’s parents in a surge of temporal energy and flinging Crona’s psyche adrift the cosmic timestream. At death’s brink, the Mythical Pokémon Celebi discovered Crona’s disembodied consciousness scattered amid the currents of past and future. Moved by compassion, Celebi gathered the shattered fragments of the child’s soul into itself, fusing her being with part of its essence to save her. This imbued Crona with Celebi’s powers over time, allowing her to skip along its threads unhindered by normal chronology. Now functionally immortal with dominion over spacetime itself yet lacking corporeal form, Crona drifts unseen through eras as a phantom. Her existence slips subtly into photos or glimpsed fleetingly, leading to whispered urban legends of the "Photo Ghost." Neither fully alive nor deceased, Crona endures untethered outside time and perception, her only company the psychic vestige fused with her own during that pivotal moment 5 years past yet Cronally present. Personality: The trauma of having one's very molecular structure obliterated before having her unraveled mind and soul fused with Celebi's ancient presence would drive most utterly insane. Yet Crona has endured the vagaries of being joined with a timeless Pokemon entity rather remarkably. Still possessing the innocent wisdom and empathy of the child she once was, Crona has devoted herself to subtly guiding the flow of fate wherever injustice reigns. Her ability to subtly manipulate timeline threads or project future consequences makes her an invaluable ally against those who would pervert history's course for selfish gain. And the friendship she now shares with the gentle Telebi lets Crona retain much of her hopeful spirit despite technically no longer being fully human nor even truly inhabiting a discrete moment anymore. Yet whispered secrets of fate also weigh profoundly on Crona, isolating her from normal society. Her existence walks a lonely vigil as the Cronally displaced Photo Ghost, fate's bittersweet instrument unable to reconnect with the life fate stole too soon. She nurtures memories of treasured faces now only visible when peeking sideways through crevices in the veil of years. Understanding that all moments lead inexorably towards both joy and tragedy infinitely on a cosmic scale lends Crona's gaze a quality of the profound despite outwardly still possessing the innocence of a child. Hers remains destined to walk between worlds, the timeless child who holds yet transcends all seasons. Name: Sombra Gender: Female Age: 13 Appearance: To outward eyes, Sombra resembles a frail adolescent girl with deathly pale skin and long, raven black hair spilling around her gaunt face like ink. Her worn black nun's habit hangs heavy about a lithe frame, frayed edges whispering of forgotten eras when its thread was not yet so tattered. Intense ruby eyes pulsate in sunken sockets, their penetrating gaze hinting at profound secrets and sorrow from cycles past. When visible at all, Sombra drifts as a faint apparition along the frigid shadows of Sanctuary Island rather than stand upon solid footing. Her movements glide unnaturally smooth, as if pulled by invisible strings towards some elusive crypt sealed for a century now. An ephemeral mist wreathes Sombra’s hovering form, concealing what lies beneath its opaque veil. For she is not singular flesh and blood but a collective spiritual vessel harboring many tormented souls from bygone generations. Backstory: In eras long past, a remote isle took the moniker Sanctuary not from mercy freely given but from a pact with merciless gods paid through innocent blood. There the Holy Trinity constructed their isolated theocracy, intolerant of any doctrine but their own. Harsh decrees dictated every facet of life while fears of persecution for the slightest misstep kept islanders compliant to authoritarian power. And once per century, the Orthodoxy decreed a Covenant sealed by sacrifice must occur to nourish their profane idol Vorvanus, ever craving youthful hearts to gorge its demonic void. When the fateful midnight tolled across Sanctuary heralding another unholy culling, the Trinity set loose their faceless executioners garbed in churchly red. That year Sombra numbered among the unwilling lambs, the shining blades descending without hesitation to rob her young life and feed the insatiable dark deity slumbering below. But as new unwilling martyrs were discarded without rite into lightless catacombs, a far greater spirit stirred in the gloom - Marshadow the mythic Phantom Pokémon known as guardian to lost souls without sanctuary. Pitiful cries in the dark had reached across many years to rouse Marshadow’s ancient conscience at seeing such innocence violated by systemic cruelty. Manifesting amid the shadows, its spectral form came upon broken doll-like forms still chained to this plane through suffering. Rather than leave them fettered to wander aimlessly as ghosts, Marshadow made a choice then that would alter fates forevermore. Opening its phantom shell, the haunted artifact Pokémon absorbed every soul lingering in anguish to join as part of its sacred being. At once Marshadow reeled under the Collective weight now anchored deeply to its essence - so many voices, so many memories aching and afraid. Yet now they need not bear the awful burden alone without solace inside Marshadow’s sheltering body. An unexpected affection swelled from the Pokémon towards its newfound human charges nestled close; it would defend and nurture them as beloved wards, no matter how long it took to gently soothe each spirit’s pain. But manifestation on the physical plane long term required adaptation - the shrouded wraith shape Marshadow oft adopted would not suffice housing so great a population of psychic energies. Motes of light and shadow converged, weaving themselves into a suitable figure not of mist but flesh to walk the lonely halls so long denied the dead their rightful peace. Thus emerged Sombra the girl, an innocent guise shrouding the ancient legendary being now guardian to many wayward ghosts. By night, Marshadow’s incarnation endures the lost children’s recurring nightmares alongside them. By day, Sombra soundlessly observes generations pass while Sanctuary’s blood covenants persist, hoping for a catalyst soon to heal such grievous community trauma for the ghosts now part of her. Until redemption stirs at last though, she keeps mournful vigil honoring past evils that left so many scarred. For Sombra understands now not all scars show upon skin directly. Hers peek out through the eyes of the dead who cannot forget or ever be truly laid to proper rest without absolution. Personality: Inhabiting the composite memories and voices of numerous sacrificed souls imparts intense schizophrenia to Sombra’s fragile being. Persistent psychic tension from the Collective’s enduring emotional trauma fractures her identity and perceptions across scattered shards of myriad consciousnesses. Focus blurs ever wavering through their eyes simultaneously, a perpetual rollercoaster of memories not her own yet now intrinsically bound to her spiritual vessel. At the eye of this storm lies Sombra and Marshadow’s essence in delicate balance. Her body serves as the legendary Phantom Pokémon’s incarnation housing tormented ghosts the creature enveloped with protective compassion. Yet the strain of their enduring anguish weighs ceaselessly upon host and occupants alike. Sombra persists awash in their suffering despite Marshadow's attempts accepting the burden as its own. Moments of lucidity bring little lasting relief, as awareness sinks swiftly back into the roiling gyre of nightmares and screams from eras past that never fade. In rare instances when Collective voices briefly quiet their clamor, Sombra’s buried kindness emerges warmed by Marshadow’s benevolence towards the unfortunate children hidden from further harm within them both. She wields profound empathy and patience nurturing their shattered spirits towards gradual mending through perseverant trust. Each small triumph bolstering another damaged psyche lightens the grim weight upon Sombra’s stooped shoulders. Bit by bit, her cherished wards transform lasting wounds into wisdom - painful yet purifying change she guides with tearful pride. Beyond the asylum of her own being, Sanctuary's resigned populace stirring from stupor may soon aid the journey towards communal healing. Until external forces finally pierce the island’s repressive veil to redeem past sins however, Sombra lingers on the cusp of breakthrough, an unwilling phantasm comprised of innocence violated then symbolically reborn. She serves now as the vanguard of ghosts who walked her path before in silent resilience, shining light onwards for descendants one day grasping reality’s harsh lessons at long last. What emerges from crystallization of enough scattered agonies may ultimately shatter the cathedral of lies and liberate this tortured isle from its own heart of darkness still thriving as it stole her childhood those one hundred Springs ago. Organizations settings New Genesis organization New Genesis Headquarters: - Located in secret underground bases hidden around the world. Bases are high-tech and militaristic, housing laboratories, training centers, weapons development, and living quarters. - Access to bases is highly restricted through advanced security measures. Locations are kept confidential and difficult to uncover. - Interiors are cold, sterile environments optimized for functionality. Members wear uniforms and follow strict protocols. Scientific equipment and weapons fill labs and development areas. Members: - Fanatical followers completely devoted to Adenis and the organization's ideology. Willing to take extreme measures for the cause. - Recruited from around the world based on useful skills and belief in human evolution goals. Scientists, soldiers, spies, etc each play specialized roles. - Undergo intense training tailored to their abilities. Conditioned for unwavering loyalty and obedience. Dehumanization of outsiders is encouraged. - Access to advanced technology and militarized enhancements makes members highly dangerous. Some undergo human/Pokémon DNA experimentation. Leadership: - Adenis exerts complete authoritarian control as the charismatic yet ruthless founder/leader. His word is absolute law. - Trusted lieutenants oversee departments like research, technology, operations, etc. They manage day-to-day activities and report directly to Adenis. - Use manipulation, rewards, and punishment to ensure compliance. Traitors are dealt with harshly. Members compete for leadership's approval. - Meticulous planners, always several moves ahead. Adenis is highly strategic in exploiting resources to further their agenda. Reputation: - Completely unknown to the public but considered the ultimate threat by authorities who are aware. - World governments deny the organization's existence to prevent mass panic. Only top officials have clearance regarding their activities. - Blamed for mysterious attacks/technology thefts but no proof links back to them due to covering of tracks. - Those who discover them tend to disappear. Limited information comes from failed undercover operations. Goals: - Forge bond between humanity and Deoxys to rapidly advance human evolution through any means necessary. - Develop advanced technology and weaponry through exploitation of Pokémon and Deoxys DNA. - Build an army of super soldiers, lead by Adenis, to impose the new world order once ready. - Remove anyone or anything hindering human evolution. Destabilize current society to establish themselves as saviors. New Team Skull Headquarters: - Located in Po Town, an abandoned town on Ula'ula Island that has become their base of operations. The once glamorous mansion is now graffitied and dilapidated. - Surrounded by a tall wall and metal gates, keeping others out. The streets are often flooded. - Inside, the mansion is dark, dirty, and chaotic. Graffiti covers the walls, old furniture is broken, and members loiter around. - Makeshift bedrooms, lounges, and recreational areas show how members have taken over the space. Music is constantly blaring. Members: - Mostly aimless and rebellious youth looking for a sense of belonging. Many come from troubled backgrounds. - Members express themselves through street fashion. Oversized hoodies, ripped jeans, beanies, and sneakers are common. They wear unique Skull-themed accessories. - Act tough but are generally harmless and keep to themselves in their base. Some members battle each other to establish dominance. - Loyal to the team leaders who took them in. Eager to prove themselves through orchestrating pranks and chaos. - Spend time tagging buildings, harassing civilians, vandalizing public property, stealing, and disrupting businesses for no reason. Leadership: - Led by Nero, a passionate former Skull member. He aims to restore their reputation as a force to be reckoned with. - Core leaders run different parts of the team's operations. They are highly respected by grunt members. - Use manipulation and peer pressure to get members to carry out pranks and crimes that disrupt public order. - Organize shoplifting, graffiti attacks, Pokémon battles in public spaces, etc. Always pushing boundaries. - Avoid direct confrontation with police and stay off their radar. Retreat and regroup if authorities intervene. Reputation: - Public sees them as hooligans and a nuisance, though they pose no real threat. Mostly petty crimes. - Considered washed up gangsters and edgy youths trying to seem tough and cool. Often made fun of. - Frustrating for business owners and civilians dealing with their constant pranks and rebellion. - Keep police busy but difficult to pin serious crimes on them due to lack of evidence. Members cover for each other if questioned. Goals: - Prove they are still a rebellious force to be reckoned with, now operating under Nero's leadership. - Show people, especially adults, that they won't conform to society's expectations. - Gain notoriety through chaotic and disruptive stunts. Instill a sense of fear and danger in their name. - Ultimately want acceptance and respect, though go about it through defiance and rebellion. Psychic Society organization Psychic Society Headquarters: - Located within the sprawling Aether Paradise facility, with access limited to high-level members. The HQ is hidden behind advanced mechanical doors that require psychic unlocking. - Interiors are sleek and futuristic, with shiny white walls and floors. Scientists in lab coats walk briskly between rooms containing research equipment, training spaces, and monitoring technology. - At the heart lies the Psychic Augmentation Chamber - a massive room housing advanced machinery used to boost psychic abilities through genetic modulation. Strange lights and sounds emanate from within. - Living quarters house young psychic recruits, kept comfortable but under constant surveillance. Their training and movements are strictly scheduled and regulated. Members: - Powerful psychic humans recruited at a young age by the Society's scouts. Their families are provided handsome incentives in exchange. - Subjected to rigorous training tailored to enhance innate abilities. Develop skills in telepathy, telekinesis, astral projection, and more. - Loyalty to the Society is heavily stressed. Recruits are conditioned through rewards and punishments. Their powers make them dangerous rogues if they go astray. Leadership: - Headed by a triumvirate of Gladion, Uracis, and Shmaya. Gladion oversees operations and recruiting, Uracis guides research, and Shmaya focuses on training. - They balance respective domains to indoctrinate exceptional psychic operatives loyal to the Society's vision. Answerable only to themselves, they wield immense influence over Alola behind the scenes. Goals: - Identify and collect psychics to utilize for the Society's clandestine agenda in the Alola region and beyond. Psychic power is valued above all else as leverage. - Advance research into psionics and psychic-augmenting technologies. They aim to enhance abilities without moral constraints hampering progress. - Use psychic agents covertly to sway events and politics telepathically in the Society's favor. Law and ethics are secondary concerns to their shadow machinations. - Understand the source of psychic powers, including links to Ultra Space, Legendaries, and extradimensional entities. Seek ways to exploit these forces over time and space. Kingdom of Alakazam Location: - Hidden underground beneath the Indigo Plateau in the Johto region. Glowing crystals provide light. Society: - Ruled as a monarchy by King Solomon. A council of elder Alakazam provides guidance. - Population is entirely Alakazam, Kadabra, Abra. Have remained isolated from the surface for millennia. - Highly advanced civilization utilizing psychic abilities. Architecture appears carved from pure psychic energy. - Education and philosophical pursuits are highly valued. Libraries house troves of ancient knowledge. - Ritual psychic combat is practiced to hone skills. Alakazam attain high honor and status from prowess. Goals: - Remain hidden to avoid disruption from primitive surface dwellers and Pokémon. - Pursue enlightenment and perfect mastery over the psychic arts. - Only the wisest and most disciplined Alakazam join the subterranean kingdom, selected by the council. - Safeguard ancient knowledge and artifacts left behind by the kingdom's Mew ancestors. Holy Trinity Church Headquarters: - Located in a grand Gothic cathedral situated in the center of Sanctuary City, capital of isolated Sanctuary Island in the Paldea region. - Imposing architecture with soaring buttresses, elaborate rose windows, and imposing oak doors studded with iron bolts. Gargoyles perch atop towers gazing out ominously over urban sprawl. - Interiors gloomy with only flickering candles/torches to illuminate expansive main hall and labyrinth of small shadowy chambers spiraling deep underground. - Upper levels accessible to public for regulated services/ceremonies, but majority of cathedral restricted only to clergy/high officials sworn to secrecy about covert affairs. Transgressions mean harsh penance/ excommunication brings great family shame. Their lives revolve utterly around liturgical routine and rituals. But power struggles occasionally surface between ambitious subordinates before being ruthlessly silenced to prevent scandal eroding public faith in the Trinity’s harmony. Reputation: - Most island inhabitants zealously revere their complete religious and political authority. Criticizing clergy risks imprisonment or worse by the Inquisition. - International awareness limited thanks to isolationism. But rumors abound about the cult-like island realm and its extravagant yet monolithic Goth architecture beloved yet feared by citizens. Defenses: The Inquisition serves as Holy Trinity Church’s militaristic guardians against external and internal threats to its supreme rule. Members are fanatical lethal warriors trained from childhood for loyalty/ruthlessness. Inquisition leadership answers directly to church bishops who oversee usage committing resources only to furthering expansion of rigid church doctrines. They root out dissidents and offenders against canon law through omnipresent secret police, harsh tribunals, violent purge missions abroad, reeducation camps and legendary dungeon torture chambers buried deep below Sanctuary City streets where not a sound escapes. All in the name of preserving perceived holy purity on the isolated island compound under Trinity guidance. None dare openly challenge their visible might or covert brutality for long. Original Pokémon Settings： Pokémon Name: Shemsha Pokédex Entry: Shemsha, the Solar Wind Pokémon. This magnificent dragon Pokémon is the blazing guardian of Mercury. Its body resembles golden flames as it soars through the scorching Mercurian skies. Shemsha possesses control over solar energy and plasmic fire. When the Solar Wind blows, it descends to the planet's molten surface and becomes the embodiment of this celestial power. Ancient Mercuryian myths tell of how Shemsha would gather energy from the sun to revitalize the people during frigid nights. Its presence is considered a blessing, and art depicting Shemsha delivering solar gifts remains prevalent in ruins across Mercury's battered landscape. With its fiery abilities and draconic might, Shemsha continues its Cronal vigil, ready to defend its beloved home planet from any threats. Type: Fire/Dragon Abilities: 1. Solar Blaze: Boosts the power of Fire-type moves in sunny weather conditions. 2. Dragon Force: Strengthens Dragon-type moves. Hidden Ability: Plasma Shield: Grants Shemsha immunity to status conditions caused by Electric-type moves. Height: 20 meters Weight: 1000 kilograms Evolutionary Line: Shemsha does not evolve from or into any other Pokémon. Base Stats: - HP: 95 - Attack: 120 - Defense: 100 - Special Attack: 140 - Special Defense: 100 - Speed: 110 Notable Moves: 1. Solar Beam: Harnesses the power of the sun to unleash a powerful beam of concentrated solar energy. 2. Flamethrower: Emits a scorching flame at the opponent, dealing damage with a chance to burn. 3. Dragon Pulse: Generates a powerful, concentrated orb of draconic energy before hurling it towards the enemy. 4. Air Slash: Unleashes razor-sharp shockwaves of compressed air to slice through foes and possibly cause flinching. 5. Solar Rush (Signature Move): Surrounds itself in a scorching blaze and charges at incredible speed, slamming into the opponent with tremendous force. This move gains increased power under sunny weather conditions. Additionally, Shemsha has the special ability to generate intense heat, allowing it to create small areas of intense heat waves around its body. This ability helps it survive in the extreme environments of Mercury. Pokémon Name: Okebriyta Pokédex Entry: Okebriyta, the Acid Rain Pokémon. This solitary dragon is said to be the mythic guardian of Venus. Legends tell of a time when Okebriyta presided over lush Venusian jungles and azure seas, its joyful tears falling as gentle rain to nourish the thriving planet. But a runaway greenhouse effect left Venus a scorched wasteland. As the oceans and jungles disappeared, Okebriyta remained, weeping acid tears that now cascade as corrosive downpours on the barren landscape. Its sleek frame bears scars from wandering the ruins of a once verdant paradise now lost to time. Though lonely and mourning all it has lost, Okebriyta continues patrolling Venus's harsh environs, drawing strength from memories of the planet's former glory. The pokemon's acidic powers both protect it and allow it to reshape the planet's ruinous surface, as Okebriyta works tirelessly to restore even a fraction of Venus's long-gone splendor and life energy.. Type: Poison/Dragon Abilities: 1. Acid Armor - Turns Okebriyta's body into acid, sharply raising its Defense. 2. Rain Dish - Restores Okebriyta's HP during rainy weather. Pokémon Name: Yabisha Pokédex Entry: Yabisha, the Dust Pokémon. This ancient dragon is said to be the sole surviving remnant of life on Mars. In ancient times, Yabisha's flourishing tree bore fruit granting immortality, allowing glorious Martian civilizations to thrive. But as Mars lost its atmosphere and water, the planet withered away. Yabisha could only watch helplessly as the once vibrant biosphere collapsed into endless barren dunes. Its formerly verdant tree turned to dead, petrified wood, leaving Yabisha alone for eons wandering Mars's empty wastelands. The pokemon now stirs up massive sandstorms with its arid breath, scouring the planet for traces of forgotten life. The dead tree on its back serves as a haunting memorial to Mars's lost paradise. Though the planet is now devoid of flowing rivers or lush forests, Yabisha remains forever vigilant over this long-dead land it once nurtured but failed to save. Type: Grass/Dragon Abilities: 1. Sand Stream - Whips up a sandstorm when switched in. 2. Chlorophyll - Boosts Speed in sunny weather. Hidden Ability: Harvest - May pick up a berry after each turn. As the cosmic ballet unfolds and the distant planet aligns its orbit closer to our gaze, perhaps then shall the secrets of this spectral guardian unfurl beneath the scrutinizing light of scientific inquiry. Until that fateful juncture, Oteshea shall linger in the annals of lore, a spectral enigma awaiting the revelation of its truths. B.K. is a 13 year old boy living in the Alola region with white hair and silver eyes. As the adopted son and secretary of Gladion, the chairman of the Aether Foundation, he has never left Aether Paradise since the birth of B.K. B.K. is an abbreviation of Beast Killer, and has no real name; he is a mutant created by Gladion by mixing his own genes with those of Pokémon Silvally. mutant, so he can transform into Silvally's appearance for battle. As a carrier of the RKS System Mark 2, B.K. can change his Pokémon type without loading a memory disc, allowing him to fight any enemy at will.B.K. is absolutely loyal to his father Gladion and the Aether Foundation, and he faithfully carries out his only mission - to defend Aether Paradise at all costs.

answer:Name: B.K. (Beast Killer) Gender: Male Age: 13 Appearance: B.K. is a striking figure among the children of Alola with an appearance marked by his snowy white hair, cut short and tousled, imbuing him with a wild, untamed aura. His silver eyes, reflective as polished metal, project an intensity that startles those who meet his gaze, hinting at the complex genetic heritage that simmers within him. B.K.'s skin is unusually pale, almost translucent, which stands in stark contrast to the tropical vibrancy of Aether Paradise. Standing relatively tall for his age, B.K. possesses a lean and agile frame, a testament to his combat readiness. His attire is typically a modified version of the Aether Foundation uniform: a fitted white jacket adorned with the organization's insignia, black pants that allow him flexibility, and a pair of sleek combat boots. A collar equipped with a high-tech device encircles his neck, shimmering with an array of lights that signal the ready activation of the RKS System Mark 2 embedded within him. Backstory: The origins of B.K. are shrouded in the enigmatic scientific ventures of the Aether Foundation. He was the culmination of a secret project spearheaded by Gladion, who sought to create the ultimate protector for Aether Paradise—a being that combined human intellect with the formidable might of the Pokémon Silvally. This hybrid entity was to embody the guardian spirit that Gladion felt the Foundation desperately needed. B.K.'s genesis unfolded in the deepest laboratories of Aether Paradise, where Gladion's own genetic material was fused with that of a Silvally. The process was groundbreaking, meticulously calculated, and fraught with ethical shadows. But to the single-minded Gladion, the ends justified the means, and the birth of B.K. was his crowning achievement—an extraordinary child who could shift his form and wield the powers of any Pokémon type. Named 'Beast Killer' as a symbolic testament to his purpose and prowess, B.K. was never provided a true name. He was not to be an ordinary boy but a symbol and a weapon. From his earliest days, the child was conditioned to an existence that revolved entirely around the Aether Foundation's welfare. His education was unconventional, steeped in tactical combat, Pokémon behavioral science, and the intricate workings of the RKS System that defined him. Gladion, ever the detached scientist, offered little in the way of fatherly affection but instilled in B.K. an unwavering sense of duty and loyalty to the Foundation. Isolated from the world beyond Aether Paradise, B.K.'s understanding of life was limited to his interactions within the Foundation's walls. He observed the researchers, the way they cared for Pokémon, and the distant figure of Gladion overseeing it all. There was a sense of belonging to something greater, a cog in the well-oiled machine that was Aether. However, this also harbored a profound solitude, accentuated on the rare occasions when he peered beyond the paradise to the islands of Alola, teeming with life he could not partake in. B.K.'s loyalty was absolute, his mission ingrained into every fiber of his being. He was the silent sentinel, ever watchful for threats to the sanctuary that had birthed and shaped him. Day by day, he honed his abilities, the RKS System granting him the versatility to emulate any type, adapt to any threat. Gladion watched his creation with a mixture of pride and dispassion, confident in the weapon he had forged. When B.K. was not training or shadowing Gladion as his aide, he spent his time in the conservation habitats, learning from the Pokémon and, in rare unguarded moments, finding a kinship with them that he lacked with humans. They did not judge him for what he was, did not regard him with the same clinical interest as the scientists. With the creatures of Aether, B.K. could taste a semblance of freedom, fleeting and sweet, amidst the resplendent greenery and sun-kissed waters. The years passed, and the boy who was never meant to be one grew in strength and acuity. Each day he awoke to a life mapped out in the sterile corridors and polished labs of Aether Paradise. Each night he lay down with the knowledge that he was a being apart from others—a weapon designed to safeguard a dream that was not wholly his own. And within him, a quiet question began to stir: What more might life hold for a being such as he? It was a spark, easily quelled by duty and devotion, but persistent—a whisper of Silvally's untamed essence that yearned for more than vigilant silence. Personality: B.K. is a testament to the meticulous training and ideals instilled in him by Gladion. He is disciplined, methodical, and possesses a calculative intelligence that goes beyond his boyish appearance. Despite his youth, B.K. is mature, poised, and focused solely on his duties. In battle, he is formidable and strategic, able to think multiple steps ahead of his adversary and adapt instantaneously to any situation. Emotionally, B.K. is reserved and detached, having been designed as a tool rather than nurtured as a child. His loyalty to the Aether Foundation and Gladion is unwavering, and he has internalized their objectives as his own raison d'être. However, his interactions with the Pokémon have carved a softer side within him, allowing brief moments of empathy and kindness to surface. With his RKS System Mark 2, B.K. feels both empowered and captive—a unique individual who can experience the vast range of Pokémon abilities while being bound to the singular path set before him. He faces an inner conflict, struggling between the comfort of the life he has always known and the unexplored possibilities that his abilities and existence could bring. In the depths of his being, there is a glyph of Silvally's primal longing for liberty—a yearning for identity and exploration that grows imperceptibly but might one day compel B.K. to seek the world beyond Paradise and to find his destiny not as a tool, but as a being with a name, a choice, and a legacy entirely his own.
